Shaping the digital future together!

<a class="link" href="https://cy.linkedin.com/company/oerotrading?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Oero Trading</a> has chosen Solvia for its digital transformation journey!

Founded in 2003, Oero Trading has turned its journey into a success story that reaches every household. With more than 30 suppliers, over 2,200 consumer products, and daily deliveries to 2,500 points, Oero connects global brands and high-quality local products with consumers.

To take this powerful operation even further, Oero is now embarking on its digital transformation journey with Solvia. 

As part of the SAP S/4HANA Public Cloud project weâ€™ve launched, purchasing, inventory and warehouse management, sales and distribution, production planning, maintenance, and financial processes will be moved to a modern cloud infrastructure. 

With this project, Oero aims to manage its supply chain in a fully integrated way, enable more efficient integration with field sales systems, increase operational efficiency, and optimize financial operations to support sustainable growth. In doing so, Oero will maintain its strong position in the distribution network while also building a future-ready, flexible, and scalable business model.

To learn more about Oero:Â <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dh6weqDW?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dh6weqDW</a>

We thank the Oero team for trusting us in their digital transformation journey and wish them great success throughout the project!
